	<div class="kadence-breadcrumbs yoast-bc-wrap"><span><span><a href="https://onebalancedlife.com/">Home</a></span> » <span><a href="https://onebalancedlife.com/recipes/">Recipe Index</a></span> » <span><a href="https://onebalancedlife.com/category/dinner/">dinner</a></span></span></div><h1 class="entry-title">Chicken Apple Sausage Sheetpan Dinner</h1><div class="entry-meta entry-meta-divider-dot">
	<span class="posted-by"><span class="meta-label">By</span><span class="author vcard"><a class="url fn n" href="https://onebalancedlife.com/author/taylorobl1102/">Taylor Dadds</a></span></span>					<span class="posted-on">

										<span class="updated-on">
						<span class="meta-label">Updated on</span><time class="entry-date published updated" datetime="2024-09-17T16:43:51+00:00">September 17, 2024</time>					</span>

<div class="entry-content single-content">
	<div class="mv-create-jtr-wrapper"><a href="#mv-creation-38-jtr" class="mv-create-jtr mv-create-jtr-slot-v2 mv-create-jtr-button mv-create-jtr-button-uppercase"><svg class="mv-create-jtr-caret" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" version="1.1"  viewBox="0 0 444.819 444.819" width="16px" height="16px"><path d="M434.252,114.203l-21.409-21.416c-7.419-7.04-16.084-10.561-25.975-10.561c-10.095,0-18.657,3.521-25.7,10.561 L222.41,231.549L83.653,92.791c-7.042-7.04-15.606-10.561-25.697-10.561c-9.896,0-18.559,3.521-25.979,10.561l-21.128,21.416 C3.615,121.436,0,130.099,0,140.188c0,10.277,3.619,18.842,10.848,25.693l185.864,185.865c6.855,7.23,15.416,10.848,25.697,10.848 c10.088,0,18.75-3.617,25.977-10.848l185.865-185.865c7.043-7.044,10.567-15.608,10.567-25.693 C444.819,130.287,441.295,121.629,434.252,114.203z"/></svg> Jump to Recipe</a></div><style></style><input class="jpibfi" type="hidden">
<p>If there&#8217;s one thing that I love during the week, it&#8217;s an easy weeknight dinner. It doesn&#8217;t get much easier than this <strong>Chicken Apple Sausage Sheetpan Dinner</strong> to fix for something easy. Plus, it makes for the perfect fall meal with some seasonal favorites like sweet potatoes and Brussels sprouts. If you want something to make when you need dinner on the table and don&#8217;t want to think about it, make this! </p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-large"><img fetchpriority="high" decoding="async" width="768" height="1024" src="https://onebalancedlife.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/Chicken-Apple-Sheetpan-Bowl-768x1024.jpg" alt="Chicken Apple Sausage Sheetpan Dinner" class="wp-image-11216" title="Chicken Apple Sausage Sheetpan Dinner " data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="I’m sure you know by now that my mix of sweet potato, Brussels sprouts and chicken sausage is my jam. " data-jpibfi-post-url="https://onebalancedlife.com/chicken_apple_sausage_sheetpan_dinner/" data-jpibfi-post-title="Chicken Apple Sausage Sheetpan Dinner" data-jpibfi-src="https://onebalancedlife.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/Chicken-Apple-Sheetpan-Bowl-768x1024.jpg" srcset="https://onebalancedlife.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/Chicken-Apple-Sheetpan-Bowl-768x1024.jpg 768w, https://onebalancedlife.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/Chicken-Apple-Sheetpan-Bowl-225x300.jpg 225w, https://onebalancedlife.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/Chicken-Apple-Sheetpan-Bowl-1152x1536.jpg 1152w, https://onebalancedlife.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/Chicken-Apple-Sheetpan-Bowl-1536x2048.jpg 1536w, https://onebalancedlife.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/Chicken-Apple-Sheetpan-Bowl-640x853.jpg 640w, https://onebalancedlife.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/Chicken-Apple-Sheetpan-Bowl-150x200.jpg 150w, https://onebalancedlife.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/Chicken-Apple-Sheetpan-Bowl-scaled.jpg 1920w" sizes="(max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px" /></figure>



<p>You know those days when dinner rolls around and you don&#8217;t know what you want to make for dinner? Or you&#8217;ve been running around all evening and need something quick to throw together that everyone will enjoy? That&#8217;s where this Sweet Potato, Brussels sprouts and Chicken Sausage Sheetpan Meal comes in. It doesn&#8217;t get much easier than this, all <em>made on one pan</em> and cooked together! You can switch it up with the chicken sausage that you prefer as there are so many different flavors! </p>



<p>This also works well as a meal prep option for the week too! If you want something that you can separate into containers and have for a couple lunch or dinners, this is a great option! It reheats easily in the microwave and I&#8217;ll enjoy it hot or cold (personal preference though!). If you want to switch up how you enjoy it, I like to top it on greens with a different sauce like hummus or a drizzle of a homemade one like the creamy jalapeno sauce below. </p>



<div id="ez-toc-container" class="ez-toc-v2_0_67_1 counter-hierarchy ez-toc-counter ez-toc-grey ez-toc-container-direction">

<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="What_you_need_for_Chicken_Apple_Sausage_Sheetpan_Dinner"></span>What you need for Chicken Apple Sausage Sheetpan Dinner: <span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h2>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li>Sweet Potatoes</li>



<li>Brussels Sprouts</li>



<li>Chicken &amp; Apple Chicken Sausage (or any of your favorites!) </li>



<li>Avocado Oil Spray</li>



<li>Sea Salt</li>



<li>Black Pepper</li>



<li>Garlic Powder</li>
</ul>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading">What you need for creamy jalapeno sauce: </h3>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li>Roasted Jalapeno</li>



<li>Plain greek yogurt</li>



<li>Lime</li>



<li>Cilantro</li>



<li>Garlic clove </li>



<li>Olive oil</li>



<li>Sea Salt</li>



<li>Black pepper</li>
</ul>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Benefits_of_a_one_pan_meal"></span><strong><em>Benefits of a one pan meal: </em></strong><span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h2>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li>Less of a mess since it&#8217;s all cooked on one pan! </li>



<li>Perfect for an easy weeknight meal </li>



<li>Can be used as prep for the week! </li>



<li>Many ways to switch them up </li>
</ul>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="How_to_make_this_sheetpan_meal"></span>How to make this sheetpan meal:<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h2>



<ol class="wp-block-list">
<li>Start by preheating the oven. You want to place your sheetpan in the oven while it is preheating! This creates optimal roasting time for your veggies. </li>



<li>Evenly chop up the sweet potatoes and brussels sprouts. </li>



<li>In a large bowl, mix together sweet potatoes and brussels sprouts with avocado oil spray, sea salt, pepper and garlic powder. Make sure the veggies are evenly coated with the avocado oil spray. </li>



<li>Lay those on the baking sheet. Be sure to give the veggies enough room </li>



<li>Place in the oven to bake for 20 minutes. Flipping half way. </li>



<li>Remove from the oven and add chicken sausage. Flip brussels sprouts and sweet potatoes. </li>



<li>Place back in the oven for 10-15 minutes. </li>



<li>Prepare jalapeño sauce for topping on veggies. </li>



<li>Enjoy! </li>
</ol>

" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://onebalancedlife.com/chicken_apple_sausage_sheetpan_dinner/" data-jpibfi-post-title="Chicken Apple Sausage Sheetpan Dinner" data-jpibfi-src="https://onebalancedlife.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/Chicken-Apple-Sheetpan-768x1024.jpg" data-lazy-srcset="https://onebalancedlife.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/Chicken-Apple-Sheetpan-768x1024.jpg 768w, https://onebalancedlife.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/Chicken-Apple-Sheetpan-225x300.jpg 225w, https://onebalancedlife.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/Chicken-Apple-Sheetpan-1152x1536.jpg 1152w, https://onebalancedlife.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/Chicken-Apple-Sheetpan-1536x2048.jpg 1536w, https://onebalancedlife.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/Chicken-Apple-Sheetpan-640x853.jpg 640w, https://onebalancedlife.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/Chicken-Apple-Sheetpan-150x200.jpg 150w, https://onebalancedlife.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/Chicken-Apple-Sheetpan-scaled.jpg 1920w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 768px) 100vw, 768px" data-lazy-src="https://onebalancedlife.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/Chicken-Apple-Sheetpan-768x1024.jpg" /><noscript><img decoding="async" width="768" height="1024" src="https://onebalancedlife.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/Chicken-Apple-Sheetpan-768x1024.jpg" alt="Chicken Apple Sausage Sheetpan Dinner" class="wp-image-11219" title="Chicken Apple Sausage Sheetpan Dinner " data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="I’m sure you know by now that my mix of sweet potato, Brussels sprouts and chicken sausage is my jam. <h2 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="What_is_the_best_way_to_store_this"></span>What is the best way to store this? <span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h2>



<p>This sheetpan meal makes for a great leftover meal! I store any leftovers in sealed containers in the fridge. I like to use <a href="https://amzn.to/3pf0zsY">these!</a> </p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Have_sheetpan_leftovers_Heres_what_you_should_do_to_reheat"></span>Have sheetpan leftovers? Here&#8217;s what you should do to reheat: <span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h2>



<p>Yay for leftovers! This is a great meal to prep extra to have for leftovers the next day or even for a couple days during the week. I like to reheat in the microwave for a minute but can also enjoy this cold.</p>

</ul>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-large"><img width="768" height="1024" decoding="async" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20768%201024'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Chicken Apple Sausage Sheetpan Dinner" class="wp-image-11222" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="I’m sure you know by now that my mix of sweet potato, Brussels sprouts and chicken sausage is my jam. " data-jpibfi-post-url="https://onebalancedlife.com/chicken_apple_sausage_sheetpan_dinner/" data-jpibfi-post-title="Chicken Apple Sausage Sheetpan Dinner" data-jpibfi-src="https://onebalancedlife.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/09/Chicken-Apple-Sheetpan-Quinoa-768x1024.jpg" data-lazy-src="https://onebalancedlife.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/09/Chicken-Apple-Sheetpan-Quinoa-768x1024.jpg" ><noscript><img width="768" height="1024" decoding="async" src="https://onebalancedlife.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/09/Chicken-Apple-Sheetpan-Quinoa-768x1024.jpg" alt="Chicken Apple Sausage Sheetpan Dinner" class="wp-image-11222" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="I’m sure you know by now that my mix of sweet potato, Brussels sprouts and chicken sausage is my jam. " data-jpibfi-post-url="https://onebalancedlife.com/chicken_apple_sausage_sheetpan_dinner/" data-jpibfi-post-title="Chicken Apple Sausage Sheetpan Dinner" data-jpibfi-src="https://onebalancedlife.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/09/Chicken-Apple-Sheetpan-Quinoa-768x1024.jpg" ></noscript></figure>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="FAQs"></span>FAQs<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h2>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading">What I used to make this sheetpan meal: </h3>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li><a href="https://amzn.to/3BI3CgJ">Baking Sheet </a></li>



<li><a href="https://amzn.to/3Phe5Yw">Parchment Paper</a></li>



<li>Avocado Oil Spray (I get mine at Trader Joe&#8217;s!) </li>
</ul>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading">Can I use regular potatoes? </h3>



<p>Yes! If you&#8217;d like to use regular potatoes instead of sweet potatoes here, you can switch it up. I would suggest red potatoes as a delicious substitute! </p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading">What are your favorite chicken sausage brands?</h3>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li>Aidells Chicken &amp; Apple Sausage (this is the one that I used here!) </li>



<li>Trader Joe&#8217;s Organic Chicken Sausage</li>



<li>Whole Foods 365 Chicken Apple Chicken Sausages </li>
</ul>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading">What are some of your favorite sauces to use? </h3>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li>Cashew Cilantro Sauce (recipe <a href="https://onebalancedlife.com/roasted-cauliflower-tostadas-2/">here</a>)</li>



<li>Trader Joe&#8217;s Jalapeno Sauce </li>



<li><a href="https://onebalancedlife.com/chipotle-basil-pesto-sauce/">Chipotle Basil Pesto Sauce</a></li>



<li>Pesto</li>



<li>Hummus</li>



<li>Bitchin&#8217; Sauce </li>
</ul>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading">Do I have to put the pan in the oven to preheat?</h3>



<p>I really recommend doing this! Since sweet potatoes and brussels can generally take a while to get a good roast, preheating the pan gives it a head start. The goal with a sheetpan meal is to have everything roast evenly and get the crisp! </p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Save_and_Pin_for_later"></span>Save and Pin for later! <span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h2>



<p>Make sure to save and pin this recipe for later! Are you <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/onebalancedlife/_created/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">following me on Pinterest</a> yet? You can also follow me on <a href="https://www.instagram.com/onebalancedlife/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Instagram</a> &amp; <a href="https://www.facebook.com/onebalancedlife" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Facebook</a>, and make sure to leave a star rating and tag me if you make this recipe! xx</p>

<h2 class="mv-create-title mv-create-title-primary">Chicken Apple Sausage Sheetpan Dinner</h2>

<div class="mv-create-times mv-create-times-3">

				<div class="mv-create-time mv-create-time-yield">
				<em class="mv-create-time-label mv-create-lowercase mv-create-strong">Yield: </em>
				<span class="mv-create-time-format mv-create-uppercase">Serves 3-4</span>
			</div>
	
						<div class="mv-create-time mv-create-time-prep">
				<em class="mv-create-time-label mv-create-lowercase mv-create-strong">Prep Time: </em>
				<span class="mv-create-time-format mv-create-uppercase"><span class="mv-time-part mv-time-minutes">15 minutes</span> </span>
			</div>
					<div class="mv-create-time mv-create-time-active">
				<em class="mv-create-time-label mv-create-lowercase mv-create-strong">Cook Time: </em>
				<span class="mv-create-time-format mv-create-uppercase"><span class="mv-time-part mv-time-minutes">40 minutes</span> </span>
			</div>
					<div class="mv-create-time mv-create-time-total">
				<em class="mv-create-time-label mv-create-lowercase mv-create-strong">Total Time: </em>
				<span class="mv-create-time-format mv-create-uppercase"><span class="mv-time-part mv-time-minutes">55 minutes</span> </span>
			</div>
			
</div>
		<div class="mv-create-description">
			<p>This one pan meal is the perfect fall meal. Filled with roasted veggies, chicken apple sausages and topped with a creamy jalapeño sauce. Meal prep this for the week or fix it for a quick dinner! </p>
		</div>
		<div id="mv-create-38" class="mv-create-reviews" data-mv-create-id="38" data-mv-create-rating="4.4" data-mv-create-total-ratings="8" data-mv-rest-url="https://onebalancedlife.com/wp-json/"></div>
	<!-- This is a button so it inherits theme styles -->
	<form class="mv-create-print-form">
		<button class="mv-create-button mv-create-print-button" data-mv-print="https://onebalancedlife.com/wp-json/mv-create/v1/creations/38/print">
			Print		</button>
	</form>
			</header>

				<div class="mv-create-ingredients">
		<h3 class="mv-create-ingredients-title mv-create-title-secondary">Ingredients</h3>

											<ul>
									<li>
						4 cups brussels sprouts, chopped					</li>
									<li>
						2 medium sweet potatoes, chopped					</li>
									<li>
						3 chicken sausages					</li>
									<li>
						Avocado Oil Spray					</li>
									<li>
						1 tsp sea salt					</li>
									<li>
						1 tsp garlic powder					</li>
									<li>
						1/2 tsp black pepper					</li>
									<li>
						1 cup quinoa, uncooked					</li>
									<li>
						optional: cilantro for topping					</li>
									<li>
						for the creamy jalapeño sauce: 					</li>
									<li>
						1/2 cup plain greek yogurt					</li>
									<li>
						1 cup cilantro					</li>
									<li>
						1 lime, juiced					</li>
									<li>
						1 roasted jalapeño					</li>
									<li>
						1 garlic clive					</li>
									<li>
						3 tbsp olive oil 					</li>
									<li>
						dash of sea salt					</li>
									<li>
						dash of pepper					</li>
									<li>
						2-3 tbsp water (for desired consistency)					</li>
							</ul>
			</div>
		<div class="mv-create-hands-free"></div>
		<div class="mv-create-instructions mv-create-instructions-slot-v2">
		<h3 class="mv-create-instructions-title mv-create-title-secondary">Instructions</h3>
		<ol><ol><li id="mv_create_38_1">Preheat the oven to 400 degrees. Add your baking sheet with parchment paper lined in to the oven to preheat too. </li><li id="mv_create_38_2">Chop sweet potatoes and brussels sprouts. You want these to be as even as possible for optimal cooking. </li><li id="mv_create_38_3">In a bowl, add brussels sprouts and sweet potatoes. Spray with avocado oil spray to evenly coat. Top with sea salt, garlic powder and black pepper. Mix together to coat. </li><li id="mv_create_38_4">Once oven is preheated, add veggies to pan leaving enough room in between them. </li><li id="mv_create_38_5">Bake for 20 minutes. Flipping half way. </li><li id="mv_create_38_6">Prepare jalape&ntilde;o sauce by adding all ingredients to a blender. Roast jalape&ntilde;o on stovetop and remove outside layer. Mix to combine. Set aside. </li><li id="mv_create_38_7">Cook quinoa according to package. </li><li id="mv_create_38_8">Take out of the oven and add chicken sausage, flip sweet potato and brussels sprouts. Spray a little avocado oil spray on chicken sausage and place back in the oven for 15-20 minutes. Flipping half way. </li><li id="mv_create_38_9">In a bowl, add cooked quinoa, chicken apple sausage sheetpan, drizzle of creamy jalape&ntilde;o sauce. Top with additional cilantro if you like. </li><li id="mv_create_38_10">Enjoy! </li></ol></ol>	</div>
	<div class="mv-create-notes mv-create-notes-slot-v2">
		<h3 class="mv-create-notes-title mv-create-title-secondary">Notes</h3>
		<div class="mv-create-notes-content">
			<p><p>I recommend using oil spray to evenly coat the veggies. </p><p>Try not to roast veggies too close to one another to prevent from steaming instead of roasting. </p><p>Evenly chopping veggies will turn out best! </p></p>
		</div>
	</div>

		</div>

		<footer class="mv-create-footer">

<h3 class="kt-adv-heading61e58f-ab wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading61e58f-ab">Hi! I'm <mark style="background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0)" class="has-inline-color has-theme-palette-3-color accent-font">Taylor.</mark> </h3>
